var servers = new Object();
function treverseMessages(node)
{
   for(var _loc3_ in node)
   {
      var _loc2_ = node[_loc3_].id;
      treveresed_safe_message_obj[_loc2_] = node[_loc3_];
      if(node[_loc3_].menu.length > 0)
      {
         treverseMessages(node[_loc3_].menu);
      }
   }
}
